I booked a seaview room but you can barely see the ocean. I'd suggest just booking a normal room,it's cheaper. My view was the pool and palm trees, which was still nice. 

I was dissapointed overall. This hotel isn't really up to par with similar well known hotels under the Marriott Bonvoy umbrella . The Sheraton is outdated. I've stayed at far better hotels that and I'd suggest booking other places. I was also dissapointed as I was made to wait 2hrs before I could enter my room after check-in. Even then my room was still being cleaned as I entered after the wait. They started cleaning after I had complained about the wait. They did apologise with a plate of fruits (which are usually complementary). The room was unfortunately non-refundable so I couldn't cancel. 

Breakfast here is good though.

Would I suggest this hotel?  Not really.

2. Then 1.2 there is no light switch on the bedside of the small bed... and there is only one socket (to plug in mosquito coils). What should I do if I want to play with my mobile phone while lying in bed? ?
3. Of course, I may not have considered letting you lie on the bed and play with your mobile phone. After all, there are two small children's beds, because the bedside is not made of soft materials and is directly on the wall. It is really difficult for you to lie on the bed and play...
4. I mentioned mosquito coils earlier. In this climate and temperature, mosquitoes are really normal. The hotel also gave us a very warm reminder that we were closing. But the problem is that the air conditioner in the room is extremely crappy. When the temperature reaches the set temperature, it stops completely and no air blows out... causing the room to feel stuffy and suffocating. If you want to continue to blow out the air, you have to continue to lower the temperature.
5. Then the combo was triggered, and the air outlet was blowing directly towards the head of the bed. 10. The hotel restaurant does not provide heating service. If you order too much food when traveling and pack it back, it cannot be heated. Of course, I didn't ask the front desk about this, but I think the restaurant doesn't provide it. I'm afraid it would be more difficult for the front desk?

The staff themselves are miserable, sitting in the lobby waiting for the airport bus at 14:15, sweating dripping down. Another failure is the air conditioner in the room, which is manually adjusted to 18¬∞C, but actually can only be maintained at 23¬∞C on the display, and the room temperature is a few degrees higher. The quilt for sleeping at night is too thick, and the hands and feet are stretched out just to be blown by the cold wind, and it is stuffy to cover under the quilt. The next day, I asked the room attendant to change two thinner quilts, which was slightly better. I'm really not afraid of thick quilts, but I'm afraid that the air conditioner is not cold enough! At the same time, justin and Xiao Wu, the housekeepers at the front desk, have a strong sense of customer service and tried their best to eliminate the dissatisfaction of the guests. They offered to change rooms, sent fruit plates, and 3 green coconuts with the Sheraton logo hot stamped as greetings. It can be seen that the hotel's top management has a high degree of authorization for front-line employees.

The hotel has Ctrip luggage delivery value-added service, free of charge, it is recommended to experience it.

The richness of hotel facilities is not as rich as Yalong Bay Tianyu, etc. At the same time, the charging items in the hotel are too eye-catching, such as: the price list in the small refrigerator in the room, the price list of several restaurants such as noodle restaurants, and the unpowered hand-operated boat by the children's pool There is also a fee, and there is a third-party popsicle cart in the lobby. A popsicle sells for 40 yuan. It is really a Rolls-Royce among popsicles. There is nothing wrong with high-priced consumption in five-star hotels, but from the perspective of geographical location and long-term perspective, it is difficult for Sheraton to have repeat customers.
